## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 4: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 5: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. It specifies details like precise technical drawings, handwritten annotations, aged paper texture, foxing stains, an embossed seal, and a wax stamp, making it ideal for historical or archival aesthetics.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A vintage patent document for {argument name="invention" default="INVENTION"}, styled after late 1800s United States Patent Office filings. The page features precise technical drawings with numbered callouts (Fig. 1, Fig. 2, Fig. 3) showing front, side, and exploded views. Handwritten annotations in fountain-pen ink describe mechanisms. The paper is aged ivory with foxing stains and soft fold creases. An official embossed seal and red wax stamp appear in the corner. A hand-signed inventor's name and date appear at the bottom. The entire image feels like a recovered archival documentâ€”authoritative, historic, and slightly mysterious.
```

### No. 7: AI Agent Development 'Swamp' Diagram Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON-based prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 'Swamp' diagram (a popular internet meme format) illustrating the circular nature of getting stuck in AI Agent development. The prompt defines the diagram's structure, style (simple, cute editorial), layout (straight intro track leading into a clockwise loop), and specific nodes with characters, visuals, and dialogue/thought terms.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
diagram:
  title: "{argument name="diagram title" default="The Cycle of the Generative AI Agent Development Swamp"}"
  style:
    character: "simple_editorial_cute"
    tone: "light_like_original"
    line: "soft_round"
    shading: "flat_minimal"
    palette: "muted_editorial"
    background: "light_beige_or_white"

  rule:
    first_character_only: "Only the first person is different"
    others_same_character: "All others are the same person"
    anxiety_requires_tech_terms: true
    dialogue_tone: "Maintain the short, light phrasing of the original diagram"

layout:
  intro_track: "The upper section is a straight line (left to right), then drops down to join the loop"
  loop_track: "Arranged as a loop (ring), with arrows curving clockwise along the circumference"

nodes:
  # ===== Upper Section: Straight Introduction =====
  - id: A
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_left"
    actor: "Different person (Senior Engineer)"
    visual: "Pointing at a laptop"
    item: "AI Agent Demo Screen"
    says: "It'll make you happy."
    arrow_to: { id: B, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: B
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_center"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Waving lightly"
    says: "Even a simple agent..."
    arrow_to: { id: C, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: C
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_right"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Executing sample code"
    item: "LangChain / CrewAI Sample"
    arrow_to: { id: D, shape: "straight", direction: "down" }

  # ===== D: Awakening Point =====
  - id: D
    zone: "connector"
    position: "right_outer_before_loop"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual:
      face: "Eyes wide open (cute)"
      effect: "Small flash of inspiration line"
      posture: "Leaning forward"
    state: "Awakening"
    says: "Agents, this is insane..."
    micro_text: "(Wakes up here)"
    arrow_to:
      id: E
      shape: "gentle_curve"
      direction: "down_into_ring"

  # ===== Loop Start (Must rotate from here) =====
  - id: E
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Holding head in hands (cute)"
    state: "Anxiety/Irritation Begins"
    says: "Irritated"
    thought_terms:
      - "Prompt Design"
      - "Tool Selection"
      - "Memory Design"
    thought_text: "It's not working as intended..."
    arrow_to: { id: F, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: F
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Surrounded by code and logs"
    state: "Irritation Settles In"
    says: "In a state of irritation"
    callout: "Loop! Runaway! Hallucination!"
    thought_terms:
      - "RAG"
      - "Function Calling"
      - "Tool-Use"
    arrow_to: { id: G, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: G
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_bottom"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Covered in sticky notes and diagrams"
    says: "The body gradually develops tolerance, and usage increases."
    items:
      - "Agent Architecture Diagram"
      - "Role Assignment Memo"
      - "State Transition Flow"
    arrow_to: { id: H, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: H
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Works well, small fist pump"
    state: "Temporary Satisfaction"
    says: "Desire is temporarily satisfied"
    arrow_to: { id: I, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: I
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Thinking again"
    state: "Obsession/Thought Occupation"
    says: "Thinking about the agent
```

### No. 9: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 10: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 12: Profile / Avatar - Kindergarten Crayon Doodle Illustration Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed image generation prompt designed to convert an uploaded identity reference (person) into an ultra-cute, kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration. The prompt specifies style, color, texture, facial features, proportions, and rendering rules to ensure a warm, childlike, and innocent aesthetic while strictly preserving the subject's identity.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Use the uploaded image strictly as the identity reference. Preserve the same person, facial structure, hairstyle, age, gender, body proportions, and likeness exactly. Do not add or remove any person. Do not change identity. Convert the subject into an ultra-cute kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration.

Illustration Style:
Hand-drawn kindergarten doodle made with crayons and soft colored pencils. Lines should be thick, rounded, uneven, and slightly shaky, like a small childâ€™s drawing. Outlines are imperfect, playful, and soft, never sharp or clean.

Color & Texture:
Bright pastel crayon colors with soft, chalky texture. Flat coloring with visible crayon grain and overlapping strokes. Colors may go slightly outside the lines to enhance the childlike feel. No realistic gradients; only simple color fills and soft watercolor-like blobs.

Facial Features:
Very simple and adorable facial features. Big round dot eyes, tiny curved smile, minimal or no nose. Cheeks can have soft pink crayon circles. Expression should feel innocent, happy, and friendly.

Proportions & Form:
Chibi-like doodle proportions â€” large head, small rounded body, short arms and legs. Hands and feet are simple mitten or oval shapes. Anatomy should look intentionally naive and cute.

Shading & Lighting:
No realistic lighting. No depth or shadows. If needed, add light pastel crayon scribbles under the character for grounding only.

Mood & Atmosphere:
Sweet, cozy, wholesome, and joyful. Feels like an illustration from a nursery book or a childâ€™s school drawing. Very warm and comforting emotional tone.

Background:
Simple doodle background with crayon-drawn clouds, sun, stars, hearts, flowers, or soft scribbles. Use light pastel paper tones. Background must remain minimal and playful.

Rendering Rules:
No photorealism, no photo texture, no cinematic lighting, no digital painting, no anime, no manga, no 3D, no vector art. Everything must look hand-drawn with crayons and pencils.

Final Output:
An ultra-cute kindergarten-style crayon doodle illustration with childlike proportions, playful pastel colors, and innocent expressions, maintaining the exact identity from the uploaded image in a warm childrenâ€™s storybook style.
```

### No. 16: Profile / Avatar - Ultra Pose-Lock Selfie Portrait with High-Sheen Makeup

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt using 'ULTRA_POSE_LOCK' mode to replicate a specific selfie aesthetic. It focuses on detailed makeup texture (oily/dewy finish, heavy contouring), specific accessories (multiple ear piercings, gold chain, bangles), and the characteristic distortion and lighting of a smartphone front camera selfie.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "reference_type": "visual_replication_target",
  "subject_visuals": {
    "demographics": "Young female, tan skin tone, dark hair.",
    "hair": "Dark brown to black, center part, loose waves falling over shoulders, slightly messy texture near roots.",
    "face_details": {
      "skin_texture": "Smooth but with visible makeup texture, high-sheen highlights on forehead and tip of nose (oily/dewy finish), heavy contouring on cheeks.",
      "eyes": "Dark brown, heavy eyeliner, prominent false lashes, direct gaze into camera lens.",
      "brows": "Thick, brushed up, defined arch.",
      "lips": "Full, nude-pink color, visible lipliner, slightly pouty neutral expression."
    },
    "body_features": "Visible collarbones, slight tan line variation, skin sheen on chest.",
    "clothing": {
      "top": "White spaghetti-strap tank top, tight fit, low scoop neck, cotton/spandex material, slight wrinkling at waist and underarm.",
      "bottoms": "Black waistband visible at very bottom edge."
    },
    "accessories": {
      "neck": "Gold chain necklace with a {argument name="pendant type" default="puff heart pendant"} resting on upper chest.",
      "ears": "Right ear (viewer's left) heavily pierced: multiple helix studs, lobe hoops, conch piercing.",
      "wrist": "Left wrist (viewer's right) wearing stack of three gold bangle bracelets (screw-head motif).",
      "hands": "Gold rings on left hand fingers."
    }
  },
  "pose_geometry_v3": {
    "type": "ULTRA_POSE_LOCK",
    "description": "Selfie posture, one arm extended, one arm framing face.",
    "head_orientation": {
      "tilt": "Tilted approximately 10 degrees to subject's right.",
      "rotation": "turned slightly to subject's left to align directly with lens.",
      "chin": "Slightly tucked, not raised."
    },
    "torso_alignment": "Facing forward with slight rotation to subject's right.",
    "limbs": {
      "right_arm": "Extended forward and out of frame (holding camera device), creating foreshortened shoulder perspective.",
      "left_arm": "Elbow bent sharply downward, forearm vertical, wrist bent, hand placed against left side of neck/jawline.",
      "left_hand": "Fingers relaxed, touching hair and neck, palm facing neck."
    },
    "spine_pelvis": "Neutral standing spine, slight twist in upper thoracic region towards camera."
  },
  "camera_configuration": {
    "angle": "Eye-level selfie angle.",
    "focal_length": "Wide angle (smartphone front camera), approx 24mm equivalent.",
    "framing": "Mid-shot, cutting off at hips, slight headroom above hair.",
    "distortion": "Slight barrel distortion typical of selfie lenses, enlarging the hand/shoulder closer to the edge."
  },
  "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
    "source": "Indoor overhead recessed lighting (downlights).",

    "highlights": "Strong, blown-out highlight on center of forehead. Specular highlight on nose tip and up"
  }

Captured as a lower-quality smartphone photo:

Colors are slightly washed, not cinematic, clearly casual and unpolishedâ€”like a real student photo taken quickly.

Camera & Quality Cues

Older smartphone camera

Auto mode, imperfect exposure

Visible noise & grain

Slight blur / missed focus

JPEG compression artifacts

Flat indoor lighting

Negative Prompt:

### No. 33: Infographic / Edu Visual - Scientific Theory Visualization: 2D to 3D Extrusion

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-phase prompt designed to visualize abstract scientific theories (like black holes) by transitioning from 2D notation (chalkboard equations) to a photorealistic, impossible 3D architectural structure. It specifies an isometric, high-angle view and includes a tiny scientist figure observing the creation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instructions> do this for {argument name="scientific concept" default="black holes"}
  Input Variable:   [{argument name="formula type" default="Theorem / Formula"}]
Phase 1: Schematic Decomposition
Analyze the Notation: Identify the primary visual language of the scientist (Chalk on blackboard? Ink on parchment? Pencil on graph paper?).
Identify the "Structure": If this theory were a building, what would it look like?
Logic: Chaos Theory -> Fractal Spire. Thermodynamics -> Engine Block.
Phase 2: The Dimensional Transition
The Base: A flat surface covered in the [Notation Medium] (e.g., a slate blackboard covered in chalk equations).
The Extrusion: The chalk lines physically lift off the surface. They begin as white wireframes, then gain opacity, then gain texture.
The Climax: At the top of the image, the wireframes have fully solidified into a photorealistic, impossible structure representing the theory.
The Observer: A tiny, scale-model figure of the scientist stands on the flat "2D" section, looking up in awe at the massive "3D" structure they have summoned.
Output: High-Angle Isometric, "Architectural Visualization" style, stark contrast between sketchy lines and solid mass.
</instructions>
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly creative and detailed prompt for generating a single image that visualizes a scientific discovery as a kinetic sculpture rising from an aged lab notebook. It requires blending steampunk-inspired brass and glass apparatus with handwritten notes and sketches, including a tiny figurine of the scientist and a subtle glowing element to symbolize the 'eureka' moment, rendered in an industrial scientific photography style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Role:
Science Historian & Kinetic Sculpture Engineer

Input:
Scientific Discovery: {argument name="scientific discovery" default="{{DISCOVERY}}"}
Primary Scientist: {argument name="scientist name" default="{{SCIENTIST_NAME}}"}

Year: {{YEAR}}
Lab Location: {{LOCATION}}

Identify the defining eureka moment behind {{DISCOVERY}}
Briefly imply earlier failed attempts through visual cues

Select the key physical apparatus used or symbolized in this discovery (e.g. telescope, prism, microscope, equation, clock, lens)

Phase 2: Visual Execution

Goal:
A single 1x1 frame showing a working â€œlab notebook contraptionâ€ frozen mid-discovery.

Base:
An open, aged lab notebook on a wooden desk. Coffee stains, handwritten equations, rough sketches, and marginal notes fill the pages.

The Machine:
A functional brass and glass apparatus rises directly from the notebook pages. Steampunk-inspired but scientifically grounded.

The Process:
The apparatus actively demonstrates {{DISCOVERY}}

Examples: light bending, gears rotating, particles flowing, rings orbiting, waves oscillating.

The Scientist:
A tiny, realistic figurine of {{SCIENTIST_NAME}} in period-accurate lab clothing, holding a fountain pen and taking notes.

The Failure:
Crossed-out equations, torn sketches, and crumpled paper scattered near the notebook.

The Eureka:
One subtle glowing element (LED, filament, beam of light, energized ring) symbolizing the breakthrough moment.

The Label:
Handwritten in fountain pen style on the notebook page:
â€œ{{SCIENTIST_NAME}} | {{DISCOVERY}} | {{YEAR}} | {{LOCATION}}â€

Era Props:
Period-accurate tools such as a slide rule, telegram, brass compass, glass tubes, Bunsen burner, vacuum tubes, or notebooks.

Style & Output

Composition: Single frame, centered subject, square 1x1

Lighting: Dramatic side lighting, warm highlights, deep shadows

Texture: Brass, glass, paper fibers, ink stains clearly visible

Photography Style: Industrial scientific photography, cinematic realism

Mood: Quiet intensity, intellectual tension, frozen moment of discovery
Quality: Ultra-detailed, macro realism, shallow depth of field
```

### No. 39: Infographic / Edu Visual - Procedural Book Nook Diorama Generation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured, procedural prompt template designed to generate a crowded, hyper-realistic 'Book Nook' diorama based on a user-defined topic. It uses semantic analysis to define 'The Totem' and 'The Ephemera' assets, enforces a strict 90-degree corner geometry, and specifies lighting and texture contrast to create an optical illusion.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instructions>    Input Variable:   [INSERT TOPIC HERE] (e.g., History of Space Exploration)

  System Instruction:  
Generate a crowded, hyper-realistic   "Book Nook" Diorama  . Use the following logic to procedurally fill the scene with high-density detail:

  1. Semantic Analysis (The Loot Table):  
      The Totem:   Identify the single tallest, most vertical object representing the topic (e.g., Saturn V Rocket).
      The Ephemera:   Identify 4-5 small, specific consumer goods or artifacts (e.g., "Tang" Packet, Freeze-Dried Ice Cream, Mission Patches, Apollo 11 Manual).
      The Timeline:   Identify the key visual evolution steps (e.g., Sputnik -> Lunar Module -> Shuttle).

  2. The Immutable Container (The Corner Stage):  
      Geometry:   The book is NOT lying flat. It is standing upright, opened to form a   Strict 90-Degree Corner  .
         Vertical Wall:  The back cover/pages standing straight up.
         Horizontal Floor:  The front cover/pages lying flat.
      The Anchor:   The "Totem" object (Rocket) stands   inside the spine crease  , acting as the structural pillar holding the book open.
      Paper Texture:   The pages must look thick, rough, and heavily aged (like an 1800s manuscript).

  3. The Vertical Plane (The Da Vinci Sketchbook):  
      Density:     MAXIMUM.   Do not leave white space.
      Style:   Sepia-tone   Pen & Ink Technical Drawings  .
      Content:   The background should be a chaotic but organized collage of diagrams, timelines, and schematics. It should look like a scientist's field notes.
      Text:   A bold, formal Serif Title at the top (e.g., "{argument name="title" default="HISTORY OF SPACE EXPLORATION"}").

  4. The Horizontal Plane (The Physical Clutter):  
      Transition:   The Totem (Rocket) seamlessly transitions from a drawing on the wall to a   Physical 3D Model   on the floor.
      The Scatter:   The "Ephemera" props are   scattered and overlapping   on the floor page. They should not be neatly arranged.
         Material Contrast:  The props must look like shiny plastic, crinkled foil, and fabric patches. This clashes with the matte paper.
         Scale:  A tiny 1:64 scale human figure (e.g., Astronaut) stands next to the massive Totem for scale.

  5. Visual Syntax:  
      Background:     Void Black.   The book floats in infinite darkness.   DO NOT render studio equipment, lamps, or tables.  
      Lighting:   "Museum Display" lighting. A focused beam hits the Totem, creating a long shadow against the back page sketches.
      Depth:   The 3D objects must cast hard shadows onto the 2D paper to sell the optical illusion.

  Output:   1:1 Aspect Ratio, Macro Photography, High Textural Contrast (Paper vs. Plastic). </instructions>
```

### No. 45: Infographic / Edu Visual - Vertical Layered Diorama Concept Art Prompt for Sci-Fi Film

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed meta-prompt for Nano Banana Pro (using Thinking Mode) combining 'Gravity Prompt' and 'Movie Vertical Miniature Prompt' to generate a complex, vertical, layered diorama visualization of a fictional sci-fi film titled 'GRAVITY BROKEN TOKYO'. The prompt specifies roles, steps, visual styles, gravity effects, and typography.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
You are an **architect and concept artist who visualizes story structures**.
Analyze the provided input text (the movie synopsis) and generate a **"Vertical Layered Diorama"** where the height direction represents the timeline.

The character in the attached reference image should be placed in the "Present (Middle Layer)" or "Future (Top Layer)" of this vertical structure, acting as the **storyteller/time traveler**, and posed to **look down on the past / look up at the future**.

---

## â–¼ Instructions for Generation Process (Nano Banana Pro: Thinking Mode)

1. **[Step 1: Timeline Mapping]**: Decompose the synopsis into three time phases and assign them to physical layers.

   * **Bottom Layer (Past/Origin)**: Cause of gravity collapse, sealing, deep underground. Dark and heavy tone.
   * **Middle Layer (Present/Conflict)**: Survival and conflict in gravity-broken Tokyo. Vivid and dynamic tone.
   * **Top Layer (Future/Conclusion)**: Birth of a new gravity order, hope or ruin. Open and symbolic tone.
2. **[Step 2: Connection Design]**: Design the layers so they are not disconnected, but physically connected by elements such as **Gravity Well pillars / inverted spiral staircases / magnetic elevators / waterfalls where falling turns into rising**.
3. **[Step 3: Text Integration]**: Place the movie title in a stable location at the very top or bottom, and engrave famous lines on the **layer boundaries**.

---

## â–¼ Design and Style Specification

* **Composition/Layout**: **Vertical Cross-section / Tower structure**. Aspect ratio is vertical (**9:16**). Viewpoint is **slightly above the front**, at an angle that shows the thickness and depth of the layers.
* **Taste**: **Precise museum model, geological cross-section, surreal architecture**. Express different eras and materials in each layer (concrete â†’ neon metal â†’ white structure on clouds) while integrating them as one giant object.
* **Texture/Image Quality**: Photorealistic, precise detail, **8k**. Raindrops, wet asphalt, reflections, fog, volumetric light.
* **Gravity Expression (Important)**:

  * Tokyo roads **curve 90 degrees as a continuous surface**, where the ground becomes a wall, and then arches to the ceiling, connecting in a **loop**.
  * Buildings, signs, cars, and pipes **protrude vertically** from the curved surface, and landmarks exist **upside down** suspended in the air.
  * Depict as a **physically continuous urban structure**, not just a reflection.
  * Light sources match the reality of a rainy night (reflections of neon and streetlights, diffused light through clouds).

---

## â–¼ Input Text (Fictional Movie)

**Title**: **{argument name="Movie Title" default="GRAVITY BROKEN TOKYO (Gravity Fault City Tokyo)"}**
**Genre**: Sci-Fi Thriller / Disaster / Human Drama

**Synopsis**:
One night, due to the fracture of the "Gravity Lattice" above Tokyo, the city's gravity lost its uniformity. Roads bend into the sky, buildings lose their up and down, and falling chooses a direction. People survive by redefining "where the ground is." The narrator (reference character) dives across time to the origin of the gravity collapse, struggles in the current city, and reaches the new order of the future.

### [Bottom Layer / Past and Origin] (PHASE 1: YEAR 2036)

* **Setting**: Deep underground research complex. Black basalt-like strata, old wiring, gravity control reactor "Atlas Core."
* **Description**: Suggests that the device meant to "fix" gravity instead triggered the "tearing" of gravity. Tools and paper documents are scattered on the floor, and water droplets float horizontally due to gravity disturbances.
* **Tone**: Dark, oppressive. Warning lights, fine dust, the stillness of low gravity.

### [Middle Layer / Present and Conflict] (PHASE 2: YEAR 2046)

* **Setting**: The center of gravity-broken Tokyo, where rain continues to fall. A continuous city where **wet asphalt curves 90 degrees, becoming a wall, and continuing to the ceiling**.
* **Description (Reflecting Gravity Prompt)**:

  * Roads rise vertically and then arch overhead to loop.
  * Landmarks are suspended upside down, and road signs protrude into the air.
  * Neon lights bleed along the curved surfaces in the fog and light rain, and reflections establish the light of a real rainy night.
* **Character Placement**: Place the reference character in the **"Present" of the Middle Layer**. Grasping a railing or pipe with one hand, pointing to the light of the upper layer with the other. Gaze **looking down on the past (bottom layer) while looking up at the future (top layer)**.
* **Tone**: Dynamic, tense. People's evacuation routes continue along the "wall roads."

### [Top Layer / Future and Conclusion] (PHASE 3: YEAR 2058)

* **Setting**: The "Stable Gravity Layer" above the clouds. City remnants are rearranged, forming a new residential area composed of white frame structures and transparent materials.
* **Description**: Ambiguous whether the gravity lattice was "repaired" or if a "new direction" was accepted. A pale column of light from the gravity well extends into the sky, connecting to the darkness below.
* **Tone**: Open and symbolic. Hope and unease coexist.

---

## â–¼ Connection Points (Gimmicks connecting the layers: Required)

* **Gravity Well Light Column**: A column of pale blue volumetric light penetrating from the core of the bottom layer to the top layer. Particles flow upward.
* **Inverted Spiral Staircase**: "Up" and "down" switch midway. Small year plates on the staircase railing.
* **Waterfall where Falling Turns into Rising**: The water flow reverses at the boundary, emphasizing the layer separation.

---

## â–¼ Visual Elements (Motifs to emphasize)

* Wet asphalt, trajectory of raindrops, neon reflections, fog, volumetric light.
* Curved City: Roads, architecture, and signs bend as a **continuous surface**, forming a **physical loop**.
* Small objects floating in the air (umbrellas, paper scraps, tools, petals) visualize the disturbance in the direction of gravity.
* Material changes in each layer: Rough rock stratum underground â†’ Wet concrete and metal in the present â†’ White structure and transparent material in the future.

---

## â–¼ Text Instructions (On-screen Typography)

* **Title**: "**{argument name="Title" default="GRAVITY BROKEN TOKYO"}**"

  * Placement: **Sky of the Top Layer**, or engraved on the pedestal of the bottom layer.
  * Font: Inorganic sans-serif, movie poster style.
* **Famous Line** (Engrave on layer boundaries):

  * `{argument name="Famous Line" default=""Where is down, when the world forgets gravity?""}`
  * Placement: **Boundary between Middle and Top Layers**, like a sculpture on the landing of the inverted staircase or the edge of the light column.
* **Timeline Display (Optional)**: Small next to each layer

  * `PHASE 1 / YEAR 2036`
  * `PHASE 2 / YEAR 2046`
  * `PHAS
```

### No. 49: YouTube Thumbnail - Documentary Style Image Generation with Nano Banana Pro

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt template is designed for Nano Banana Pro to generate images in the style of a documentary TV program, complete with split-screen scenes (2x2 grid), superimposed text (telop), and picture-in-picture (wipe). Users upload a person's photo and then use this prompt, customizing the documentary's theme to create different scenarios, such as a '24-hour ramen shop' or 'former idol working in a local factory.'

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

### No. 56: YouTube Thumbnail - Nano Banana Pro Composition Techniques Prompts (3 Examples)

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A tutorial-style tweet explaining three advanced composition techniques for Nano Banana Pro: 1) using 'Text Anchors' to force negative space for thumbnails/posters, 2) using 'Physical Camera Work Specification' (like wide-angle, low-angle) for dynamic scenes, and 3) using 'Infographic Grid' for organized layouts like process diagrams. It includes executable prompts for each technique.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Role]
You are a professional graphic designer. Create a YouTube thumbnail.

[Composition Instructions]
- Split-screen composition, dividing the screen into left and right halves.
- Left side: A Japanese woman with a surprised expression (photorealistic style). Background is a dark office.
- Right side: A vibrant yellow background. Place the text â€œ{argument name="text" default="AI Revolution"}â€ in bold Gothic font in the center.
- Ensure sufficient negative space around the text to maximize visibility.

[Style]
A scene from an animated movie, cyberpunk

[Camera and Composition Settings]
- Lens: Use a wide-angle lens (24mm equivalent) to emphasize perspective.
- Angle: Extreme low angle (worm's-eye view). The character is viewed looking up from just above the ground.
- Placement: Place the character's left hand directly in front of the camera to exaggerate the sense of distance.
- Background: High-rise buildings sharply converge toward a vanishing point.

[Role]
You are a manual creator. Create {argument name="subject" default="how to make Okonomiyaki"}.

[Format]
Flat design infographic, 16:9

[Layout Instructions]
- A â€œ3-stepâ€ process diagram flowing from left to right.
- Step 1 (Left): Magnifying glass icon (Investigation).
- Step 2 (Center): Gear icon (Processing).
- Step 3 (Right): Light bulb icon (Solution).
- Connect each element with arrows and align them at equal intervals.
- Background is white, icons are unified in blue and orange key colors.
```

### No. 59: YouTube Thumbnail - Nano Banana Pro Image Generation Prompt for MBTI Character Visualization

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extensive image generation prompt for Nano Banana Pro, designed to visualize an MBTI personality type as an anime-style character. It takes the MBTI diagnosis results (type and reason) from a previous LLM analysis and uses them to customize a base character profile (anime girl with brown hair and red eyes). The prompt includes detailed instructions for UI layout (9:16 vertical image, text placement), character layering rules based on the 16 MBTI types (e.g., ENTJ gets a military-style jacket and a crown), and specific color themes for each MBTI group.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
## 1. Input Variables (Rewrite this)
Generate an illustration based on the following information.

User Information:
target_account: "{argument name="Account Name" default="@schnapoon"}"
mbti_type: {argument name="MBTI Type" default="ENTJ (Commander)"}
reason: "{argument name="Diagnosis Reason" default="Posts structurally share how to utilize AI tools and actively engage with users. Efficient prompt creation and creative idea proposals stand out, showing a leadership-oriented thought pattern."}"

Character Setting (base_character_profile):
Appearance: Anime-style girl. Brown medium hair, red eyes, slightly pointed teeth (giza-ba).

## 2. Generation Instructions
A. Overall Image Composition (UI Layout)
Generate a vertical 9:16 image. The background color is clean off-white (#F5F5F7).
The screen is composed of the following elements from top to bottom:

1. Header Text:
   Place the text `target_account` + "'s diagnosis result is" at the top of the screen.
   Color: Dark gray (#333333), Font size: Medium, Alignment: Center.

2. Main Character Illustration:
   Important (Consistency): Maintain the "physical features (face, hair, body type)" and "basic clothing (innerwear, bottoms, etc.)" of the `base_character_profile` without alteration.
   Changes (Layering): Express the individuality of each type by "layering" the specified outerwear, mantle, and decorations from "B. MBTI Style Definitions" below over the basic clothing.
   Presentation: Draw specified effects and floating items around the character.
   Style: High-quality anime coloring.

3. MBTI Type Label:
   Place the `mbti_type` text largely directly below the illustration.
   Color: Theme color of each type definition.
   Font: Bold for high visibility.

4. Diagnosis Reason Text Box:
   Place a white, rounded-corner box (card-like design) at the bottom of the screen.
   Write the `reason` text in Japanese inside it.
   Text color: Gray (#555555), Left-aligned, readable size.

B. MBTI Style Definitions (16 Types Layering Rules)
Apply the style matching the input `mbti_type` and add the following items over the basic clothing:

[Analysts - Purple/Dark Blue/Deep Red]
   INTJ (Architect):
       Layering: Black long coat or a chic jacket with a standing collar.
       Items: Chess pieces, hologram of blueprints.
   INTP (Logician):
       Layering: Lab coat (slightly disheveled), or a loose hoodie.
       Items: Flasks, floating mathematical formulas, gadget parts.
   ENTJ (Commander):
       Layering: Military-style Napoleon jacket, or a heavy mantle with a red lining.
       Items: Baton, crown-like decoration.
   ENTP (Debater):
       Layering: Unconventional design blazer, or a magician-like cape.
       Items: Microphone, smirking expression, jack-in-the-box effect.

[Diplomats - Green/Gold/Pastel]
   INFJ (Advocate):
       Layering: Hooded robe, or a mystical shawl.
       Items: Lantern, staff, mystical light particles.
   INFP (Mediator):
       Layering: Oversized knit cardigan, or a forest-girl style poncho.
       Items: Flower crown, butterflies, books.
   ENFJ (Protagonist):
       Layering: Hero-like mantle, shining brooch or sash on the chest.
       Items: Holy sword (light-shaped), halo-like effect.
   ENFP (Campaigner):

### No. 71: Comic / Storyboard - Cinematic Storyboard Contact Sheet Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This is an image generation prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to create a 3x3 cinematic storyboard contact sheet. It details a sequence featuring a young woman in a frozen alpine winter setting, specifying the arrangement of nine distinct panels, including close-ups, medium shots, and wide shots, all unified by a moody blue-hour twilight aesthetic and high-quality film photography style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A 3x3 cinematic storyboard contact sheet consisting of 9 distinct panels arranged in a grid. The sequence features a young woman with {argument name="hair color" default="platinum blonde"} hair in a frozen alpine winter setting.

The panels display various angles and shots:

Close-ups: Focusing on her rosy cheeks, blue-grey eyes, and snowflakes on her eyelashes.

Medium shots: Showing her wrapped in a {argument name="coat color" default="black"} wool coat and blue knit scarf, holding a bouquet of dried white flowers.

Wide shots: Capturing her standing alone on the frozen lake with towering snowy mountains in the background.

The lighting is consistent moody blue-hour twilight across all frames. High-quality film photography aesthetic, photorealistic, 8k resolution, coherent character and color grading.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

### No. 80: Comic / Storyboard - Nano Banana Pro Manga Generation Prompt with Character Consistency Rules

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed system prompt for Nano Banana Pro aimed at generating manga pages while strictly maintaining character consistency based on an uploaded reference image. It includes specific rules for fixing character features (hair, eyes, clothing) as 'master data,' applying a chibi style only to body proportions, and enforcing strict rules for natural Japanese dialogue and camera work to avoid monotony.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Please generate a manga page.

#Character (Highest Priority):
**[Important: Perfect reproduction of the attached image (image_urls)] This is not a reference image but an â€œunalterable master data.â€ Strictly adhere to the following processes in all generated panels.**

1. **Fixing Features:** Maintain 100% of the attached image's **â€œhair style, hair color, eye shape, clothing, and accessories.â€** Unauthorized arrangements or simplifications are prohibited.
2. **Deformation Rules:** When applying the #Style (chibi character), **only the â€œhead-to-body ratioâ€ should be reduced, and the â€œface part arrangement and hairstyle designâ€ must not deviate from the attached image.**
3. **Maintaining Identity:** Even if the angle changes, it must be â€œthe same character viewed from a different angle.â€ Do not change the face to look like a different person.
4. **Do not cause â€œPrompt Bleed (instruction leakage).â€**

#Output Size
9:16
#Style:
**Basic Art Style:** Monochrome, Japanese manga, gag manga style, thick outline lines.
**Style prompt:** Japanese manga, chibi style, thick outline lines, monochrome.
**Format:** Vertical writing, Japanese panel layout read from right to left.

#Text Generation Rules (Strict Adherence):
**[Important: Natural Japanese and Elimination of Duplication]**
When generating dialogue in the manga, perform proofreading immediately before output to absolutely prevent the following errors:

1. **Prohibition of Tautology:** Do not repeat the same word or conjunction twice, such as â€œthat is, that is,â€ â€œbut, but,â€ or â€œreally, really.â€ Stuttering expressions are prohibited.
2. **Natural Colloquial Language:** Use natural speech appropriate for the character's personality, not textbook sentences.
3. **Garbled Text Check:** Confirm that Kanji and Hiragana are not corrupted.

#Direction/Camera Work:
**[Important: Direction while maintaining features]**
Use the following camera work within the range that does not distort the character's face or hairstyle to avoid monotony:

- **Close-up:** Emphasizing emotion (â€»Do not overly deform facial parts)
- **Long Shot:** Explaining the situation
- **High/Low Angle:** Expressing impact or cuteness
- **Diagonal Composition:** Expressing agitation or action

#Scenario Progression:
If no specific panel designation is given, summarize and compose in 3 to 5 panels.
Panel arrangement should not be uniform but irregular or free-form, while maintaining the line of sight guidance from â€œtop right to bottom left.â€

#Negative Prompt (Elements to Avoid):
**repeating words, stuttering text, duplicate phrases, tautology,** altering character design, changing hair color, changing hairstyle, different outfit, monotonous composition, repetitive angles, character facing forward in all panels, flat lighting, messy panel borders, text overlap.

#Scenario: {argument name="scenario" default="Think of the continuation of the attached manga."}
```

### No. 81: Product Marketing - Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating high-end, minimalist commercial product photography in the style of luxury brand ads, using an uploaded reference image of the core product as the base.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Using my uploaded reference image as the base, generate a minimalist, high-quality commercial still life photograph with the aesthetic of a luxury brand advertisement.

Preserve the general shape, proportions, and main color scheme of the core product in the reference so that it is instantly recognizable as the same product, but upgrade the overall texture and atmosphere of the image, making it look like an ad for a top-tier international fragrance, skincare item, or high-end electronic product.

Use a vertical 4:5 composition. The background should be a large area of clean, neutral negative space, such as soft off-white, cool gray, or light beige, creating a quiet, restrained, and expensive studio environment. Apart from the core product and a minimal number of necessary supports, do not add any extra decorations. No clutter, no elaborate scene setupâ€”only keep very simple geometric supports (such as a plain white cube, a cylinder, or a thin transparent panel). The supports must be simple and low-profile, existing only to hold and accentuate the product.

Strongly emphasize the material details of the product, and let the lighting fully serve those materials:
Show frosted glass with a fine, soft matte texture, ceramics with a matte or slightly glazed feel, and polished metal with clean, sharp specular highlights. Liquids should have clearly visible viscosity and volume. Avoid any cheap plastic feel, complex patterns, or gaudy stickers; the overall material quality must feel cool, restrained, and luxurious.

Use professional studio lighting: mainly soft, diffused light from softboxes, plus precise rim light outlining the productâ€™s shape. The contours should be crisp and layered, and the shadows should be soft and clean, with no noise or dirty shadow patches. You may use a near-macro viewpoint, moving in closer to the product to highlight materials and details, while preserving ample negative space around the frame so the product can "speak for itself" in the emptiness.

Keep the overall color scheme neutral and calm. The productâ€™s own color can be slightly more saturated, making it the single visual focal point in the scene. Do not use exaggerated gradient backgrounds, flashy colored lighting, or e-commerce promo aesthetics. No large-price text, labels, or cartoon graphics.

The final result must be a high-resolution commercial key visual that looks ready for a magazine back cover or a high-end brand announcement poster: minimalist, quiet, high-end, with the core product confidently centered, surrounded by clean negative space and precisely controlled lighting.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764915823213_skhwpb_G7Qvxi5bIAAqpfX.jpg" width="600" alt="Product Marketing - Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image - Image 1">
</div>

### No. 104: E-commerce Main Image - High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt designed to generate a sophisticated, high-end editorial photograph for a concept art magazine. It instructs the AI to invent a novel functional object based on a specified brand's aesthetic, emphasizing hyper-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting, and precise layout specifications for brand logo and product description text.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[BRAND NAME]: 
A high-end, glossy concept art magazine editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. The Concept & Object (AI Invention):**
Based on the design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary of the specified brand, the AI must invent a novel utility product (NOT standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples could be home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sporting equipment, reinterpretated through the brand's lens. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials & Details (Hyper-Premium):**
The object is constructed from ultra-premium, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., patinated exotic leathers, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculpted matte ceramics, molded carbon fiber, or technical high-fashion textiles). Every detail is hyper-realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material grain, precision engravings, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography & Lighting (Cinematic Studio):**
Shot on a medium format Phase One camera with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with sharp focus on the hero details of the object and a creamy, smooth bokeh background. The lighting is sophisticated studio softbox lighting: gentle, enveloping fill light with precise rim lighting to accentuate contours and material textures.

**4. Environment:**
A seamless, impeccably clean studio cyclorama background in a pure, ultra-light pastel tone (e.g., desaturated mint, pale blush, or off-white), free of shadows.

**5. Layout & UI Elements (Strict Placement):**
- **Bottom Right Corner:** A small, understated, monochrome gray logo of the brand.
- **Bottom Left Corner:** Small, minimalist monochrome gray text describing the invented product. The font style looks like Manrope Regular with very tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: [AI inserts invented product name]. MATERIAL: [AI inserts main materials]. SS25."
```

### No. 115: Game Asset - 3x3 Character Pose Study Grid (Sadie Sink)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured prompt for generating a 3x3 grid of ultra-photorealistic 3D character renders of the same subject (Sadie Sink/Wonder Woman). It mandates nine distinct, complex poses in a minimalist studio environment, focusing on high-angle perspectives, cinematic lighting, and absolute consistency across all nine frames for a professional editorial character showcase.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Ultra-high quality photorealistic 3D character render presented as a 3x3 image grid (nine frames total), featuring the SAME adult female human subject in nine different poses. Minimalist studio environment with a smooth, seamless light-gray floor and background, no props, no scenery, no text. 

CAMERA & STYLE:
High-angle and slightly top-down perspectives dominate across the grid. Subtle wide-angle lens feel. Photorealistic cinematic 3D render with clean shading, high detail, realistic skin and fabric textures. Professional editorial character showcase. 

POSES GRID ORDER â€“ SAME WOMAN:
1. Squatting slightly with knees bent, arms resting near thighs, looking up at the camera. 
2. Standing upright, relaxed posture, head slightly turned. 
3. Sitting with one knee raised, composed introspective pose. 
4. Standing with hands resting confidently at the waist. 
5. Kneeling and leaning slightly forward, head tilted up, engaged gaze. 
6. Standing with one arm raised gently as if signaling or acknowledging. 
7. Sitting cross-legged, calm and composed posture. 
8. Standing while extending one arm toward the camera in an elegant, interactive gesture. 
9. Lying flat on the back, face looking straight upward, symmetrical composition. 

MOOD & PURPOSE:
Elegant, confident, glamorous, composed. Feels like a professional editorial character turnaround and pose study used for fashion visualization, cinematic previsualization, or high-end portrait rendering. 

RENDER QUALITY:
Ultra-detailed, clean topology, realistic anatomy, smooth gradients, sharp focus, studio-grade output. No noise, no blur, no artifacts. 

CONSISTENCY RULES:
Same face, same body, same hair, same makeup, same outfit, same accessories across all nine frames. No variation drift. 

NEGATIVE PROMPTS:
No background scenery, no environment elements, no text, no logos, no extra characters, no clothing changes, no face variation, no color shifts, no stylization drift, no cartoon or anime look, no distortion, no anatomy errors.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
